***простаивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:простаивать.html>проста́ивать</a> (20863)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простоять.html>простоя́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prostojátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простаивать.html>проста́ивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prostáivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простоять.html>простоя́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stand, to stay <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">for some time</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to stand idle</li>
<li>to stand, to remain <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">for buildings</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простенок.html>просте́нок</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prosténok</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простенок.html>просте́нка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простенок.html>просте́нки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простенок.html>просте́нков</a></b>)

***простереть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:простереть.html>простере́ть</a> (31247)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">прострѣти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prostrěti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (first singular <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">простьрѫ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prostĭrǫ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">про̀стриjети</i> (first singular <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">про̏стриjе̄м</i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">prostrẹ́ti</i> (first singular <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">prostrèm</i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">prostříti</i>, etc.
</p><p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*prosterti</i> (first singular <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*prostьrǫ</i>), composed of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pro-</i> + |  <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sterti</i>, cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">स्तृणाति</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stṛṇā́ti</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sprinkle, throw</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">स्तृणोति</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stṛṇṓti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">स्तरति</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stárati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Avestan" class="extiw" title="w:Avestan">Avestan</a></span> <i class="Avst mention" lang="ae">𐬯𐬙𐬀𐬭𐬀𐬌𐬙𐬌</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ae-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">staraiti</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to stretch out</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latvian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Latvian language">Latvian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">stirinât</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to move, shake</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">στόρνῡμι</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stórnūmi</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to spread</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">στορέννῡμι</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">storénnūmi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">στρώννῡμι</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">strṓnnūmi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">sternō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to spread out</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Past passive participle <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*prostьrtъ</i> is an exact cognate of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Avestan" class="extiw" title="w:Avestan">Avestan</a></span> <i class="Avst mention" lang="ae">𐬟𐬭𐬀𐬯𐬙𐬆𐬭𐬆𐬙𐬀</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ae-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">frastərəta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, and base form <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*stьrtъ</i> is an exact cognate of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">स्तृत</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stṛtá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">στρωτός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">strōtós</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">strātus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простереть.html>простере́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prosterétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простирать.html>простира́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stretch, to extend, to hold/reach <i>(out)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:простереть.html>простере́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prosterétʹ</b> rúki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to raise [hold / reach out] one's hands</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:простецкий.html>просте́цкий</a> (25561)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простой.html>просто́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prostój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ец</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ec</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-цкий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ckij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простецкий.html>просте́цкий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prostéckij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> basic, simple, modest</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> simple, easygoing</li></ol>

***простирать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:простирать.html>простира́ть</a> (26378)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-стира́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-stirátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, imperfective equivalent of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-стере́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sterétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (see <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простереть.html>простере́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prosterétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>); compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тира́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-tirátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, imperfective equivalent of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тереть.html>тере́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">terétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> in prefixed verbs.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простирать.html>простира́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prostirátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простереть.html>простере́ть</a></b>)

***простираться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:простираться.html>простира́ться</a> (11756)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простирать.html>простира́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prostirátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to stretch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простираться.html>простира́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prostirátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">простере́ться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stretch, to reach, to range
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:простираться.html>простира́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> чего́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prostirátʹsja</b> do čevó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to reach something; stretch to something</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:простираться.html>простира́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сто.html>сто</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:километр.html>киломе́тров</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prostirátʹsja</b> na sto kilométrov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to stretch for a hundred kilometres</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простирать.html>простира́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prostirátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to stretch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проституция.html>проститу́ция</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prostitúcija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проституция.html>проститу́ции</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проституция.html>проститу́ции</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проституция.html>проститу́ций</a></b>)

***простить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:простить.html>прости́ть</a> (781)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">простити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prostiti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from Proto slavic root <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*prostъ-</i>. Cognate to <a href = vnd.unilang:простой.html>просто́й</a>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простить.html>прости́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prostítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прощать.html>проща́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to excuse, to forgive, to pardon</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:извинить.html>извини́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">izvinítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простить.html>прости́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prostítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проститься.html>прости́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prostítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прощаться.html>проща́ться</a></b>)
</p>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простодушный.html>простоду́шный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prostodúšnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>openhearted, simple-hearted, simple-minded, artless, unsophisticated</li></ol>

***простой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:простой.html>просто́й</a> (445)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">простъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prostŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*prostъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простой.html>просто́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prostój</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)про́ще</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простейший.html>просте́йший</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>simple, ordinary</li>
<li>basic</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> prime</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простак.html>проста́к</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prosták</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простота.html>простота́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prostotá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упрощать.html>упроща́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">uproščátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упрощение.html>упроще́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">uproščénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простаивать.html>проста́ивать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prostáivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простой.html>просто́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prostój</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простой.html>просто́я</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простой.html>просто́и</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простой.html>просто́ев</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>standstill, stoppage, idle time, downtime</li></ol>

***простолюдин.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:простолюдин.html>простолюди́н</a> (22070)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">простълюдинъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prostŭljudinŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; see <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простой.html>просто́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prostój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>лю́ди</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ljúdi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простолюдин.html>простолюди́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prostoljudín</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простолюдин.html>простолюди́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простолюдин.html>простолюди́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простолюдин.html>простолюди́нов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>commoner</li></ol>

***простонать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:простонать.html>простона́ть</a> (10288)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стонать.html>стона́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stonátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простонать.html>простона́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prostonátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стонать.html>стона́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to groan, to moan <i>(for a certain time)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:больной.html>больно́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:простонать.html>простона́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ночь.html>ночь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bolʹnój <b>prostonál</b> vsju nočʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the patient was groaning all night</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to utter a groan/moan</li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стон.html>стон</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ston</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:застонать.html>застона́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zastonátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***простор.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:простор.html>просто́р</a> (4131)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*prostorъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простор.html>просто́р</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prostór</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простор.html>просто́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простор.html>просто́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простор.html>просто́ров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>open space, expanse</li>
<li>freedom</li>
<li>scope, range</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:просторечие.html>просторе́чие</a> (25768)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простой.html>просто́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prostój</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ordinary</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:речь.html>речь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rečʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">speech</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ие</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:просторечие.html>просторе́чие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prostoréčije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:просторечие.html>просторе́чия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:просторечие.html>просторе́чия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:просторечие.html>просторе́чий</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">просторе́чный</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">linguistics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> an informally spoken idiom that is considered to be non-standard <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">often related to uneducated people</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>; vernacular speech
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повелительный.html>повели́тельные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рмы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́ла</a> «<a href = vnd.unilang:ехать.html>е́хать</a>» - е́хай, е́хайте, едь, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> е́дьте. <a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>они́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:присущий.html>прису́щи</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:просторечие.html>просторе́чию</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Povelítelʹnyje fórmy glagóla “jéxatʹ” - jéxaj, jéxajte, jedʹ, i jédʹte. Oní prisúšči <b>prostoréčiju</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The imperative forms of the verb <a href = vnd.unilang:ехать.html>е́хать</a> are е́хай, е́хайте, едь, and е́дьте. They are inherently vernacular.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Являясь идиомом, органически связанным с говорами, <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">просторечие</span> не может быть полностью лишено территориального варьирования, при этом оно, безусловно, территориально варьирует сильнее литературного языка. </span></li>
</ul></li>


<li>простой язык, обиходно сниженная речь, содержащая непринужденные и несколько грубоватые слова и формы языка, не входящие в норму литературной речи <span class="example-fullblock example-absent-block"><ul>
</ul></li>

</ol>

</p>
<ol><li>spaciously
<ul><li><div class="wiktQuote" data-validation="white"><a href = vnd.unilang:лев.html>Лев</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:толстый.html>То́лстой</a>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:хозяин.html>Хозя́ин</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работник.html>рабо́тник</a></i> 1895:<dl><dd><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">- то́-то <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>тебе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хозяин.html>хозя́ином</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:просторный.html>просто́рно</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:гулять.html>гуля́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бу́дет</a> - <a href = vnd.unilang:сказать.html>сказа́л</a> ники́та</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">- tó-to tebé s xozjáinom <b>prostórno</b> guljátʹ búdet - skazál Nikíta</i></dd><dd>-so, you and the landlord will walk <b>spaciously</b> around</dd></dl></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>стоя́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stojátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>to stand, to stay <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">for some time</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>

<li>to stand, to remain <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of buildings</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***пространный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пространный.html>простра́нный</a> (14736)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Based on the same root as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пространство.html>простра́нство</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prostránstvo</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">space</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:странствие.html>стра́нствие</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stránstvije</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wandering</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пространный.html>простра́нный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prostránnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> extensive, vast</li>
<li>diffuse, verbose, wordy</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пространственный.html>простра́нственный</a> (14146)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пространство.html>простра́нство</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prostránstvo</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">space</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-енный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пространственный.html>простра́нственный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prostránstvennyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>spatial</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пространство.html>простра́нство</a> (1032)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">пространьство</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prostranĭstvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*prostornьstvo</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:страна.html>страна́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">straná</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">country, region</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ство</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-stvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пространство.html>простра́нство</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prostránstvo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пространство.html>простра́нства</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пространство.html>простра́нства</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пространство.html>простра́нств</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>space (intervening contents of a volume)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:общественный.html>обще́ственное</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пространство.html>простра́нство</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">obščéstvennoje <b>prostránstvo</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">public space</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>spacing, space, gap, distance between two points</li></ol>
